                            n="2"/>bhighātopadrutān āsanāthān anāthavad viceṣṭamānān vikrośataś ca

                        āmuṣmikañ ca śreyas tad bhagavantam upasannā sma | śiṣyatveneti </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.1.5">tān uvāca bhagavān svāgatam vaḥ sava evāmīmāṃsyā a<lb n="3"

                        anutpādyaiva ca prajāḥ ślokaśatasahasram adhyāyasahasrañ ca kṛtavān

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.16"> parilihed uttaroṣṭham uṅgarāṃś ca karoti vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         pretair vā bhāṣate sārdhaṃ sa parā<cb n="1"/>sur asaṃśayaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.17"> khebhyaḥ saromakūpebhyo yasya raktaṃ pravarttate |
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣasyāviṣārttasya sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.18"> vātāṣṭhīlā <cb n="2"/>tu hṛdaye yasyorddham anuyāyinī |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujānnavidveṣakarī sa parāsur asaṃśayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.19"> ananyopadravakṛtaḥ pā<lb n="7"/>daḥ śophasamutthitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣaṃ hanti nārīñ ca mukhajo guhyajo dvayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.20"> atīsāro jvaro dhmānañ chardiḥ <cb n="1"/>s<unclear
                            reason="faded">ū</unclear>nāṅgameḍhratā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kāsina svāsino vāpi yasya taṃ kṣīṇam ādiśet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.21"> svedo dāhaś ca balavāṃ hikkā svāsaś ca mānava<unclear
                            cert="medium" reason="faded">ṃ</unclear> |
                        <caesura/>
                         bala<cb n="2"/>vantam api prāṇair viyujanti na saṃśaya<unclear
                            cert="medium" reason="faded">ṃ</unclear> | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.22"> syāvā jihvā bhaved yasya savyañ cākṣi nimajjati |
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhañ ca <pb n="26v"/><lb n="1"
                        /><!-- A45-05+73274+029.jpg --><!-- A1267-11+103612+063.jpg -->jāyate pūtir
                        yasya taṃ parivarjayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.23"> netre cāsyena pūryete svidyete caraṇau tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         cakṣuś cākulatāṃ yāti ya<cb n="1"/>marāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.24"> atimātra laghūni syur gātrāṇy atigurūṇi vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         yasyākasmāt sa vijñeyo gantā caiva yamālayaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.25"> paṅkama<cb n="2"/>tsyavasātailaghṛtagandhāṃś ca ye narāḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṣṭagandhāṃś ca y<subst><del rend="erased">o</del>
                            <add>e</add></subst> vānti gatās te yamasādanaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.26"> yūkā lalāṭam āyā<lb n="2"/>nti balin nāśnānti vāyasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yeṣāñ cāpi ratiṃ nāsti gatās te yamasādanaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.27"> jvarātīsāraśophā syur yasyā<cb n="1"/>nyonyāvasādinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣīṇañ ca balaṃ yasya na sa śakya cikitsituṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.28"> kṣīṇasya yasya kṣuttṛṣṇe hṛdyair mṛṣṭair hitais tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         annapānai<cb n="2"/>r na śāsyeta tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.29"> pravāhikā śiraḥśūlaṅ koṣṭhaśūlaś ca dāruṇam |
                        <caesura/>
                         pipāsā balahāniś ca <lb n="3"/>tasya mṛtyur upasthitaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.30"> viṣameṇopacāreṇa karmabhiś ca purākṛtaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anityāc ca jaṃtūnāṃ jīvitan nidha<cb n="1"/>nam vrajet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.31"> pretā dūtā piśācāś ca rakṣāṃsi vividhāni ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         maraṇīyan naran nityam upasarpanti sarvadā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.31.32"> tāni bheṣajavīryāṇi prati<cb n="2"/>nighnanti sarvadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt mohā kriyā sarvā bhavantīha gatāyuṣam iti ||31 || </l>
